msg:Transportation: Very convenient, opposite to the hotel is Zhuzilin Station of Metro Line 1 (Exit B2). It takes only 5 minutes to get there, but there is a long corridor in the subway.

Room environment: For this three-person trip, we will book the left deluxe twin room (for 4 people). There are two 1.8-meter-large beds in the room, and there is also a beautiful city view, and you can also see some sea views. The rooms are very clean.
But because the hotel has been in operation for many years, the sofa is a little old, the picture quality of the TV is low, and the remote control is more difficult. There are 2 USB chargers in the room, and more than three plugs. You can choose between bathtub and bathtub in the bathroom. The bathtub is a little dirty, but there are only two sets of towels, slippers and toothbrushes in the four-person room, so you need to call the front desk and ask for more sets.
In terms of Wi-Fi, it is not used at all. Although it shows that it is connected on the left and the signal is good, it is completely loaded and cannot be accessed anywhere.

Hotel facilities: I went to the left indoor swimming pool today. There are relatively few people swimming in the pool, and the pool area is quite large, so it is very comfortable to swim. However, the top of the interior is quite dirty, with a lot of rust, and the appearance is not very good. The Continental Hotel requires guests to wear a swimming cap before they can enter the swimming pool, otherwise they have to buy it in the hotel. Overall, the price/performance ratio is high, and everyone in the house is very satisfied.
